<s> the little crooked old man in the window seat who had been witnessing the fencing match between the two gentlemen whose stamping and jumping had been such as to cause him to give up all attempts to continue writing the theatre music in the copying of which he had been engaged looked up eagerly towards the new comer as the major of the well blacked boots entered the apartment distributing the most graceful bows to everybody present <\s>
<s> me daughter me friend mr <\s>
<s> bows me gallant young pupil and friend i may call um sir derby oaks said costigan splendidly waving his hand and pointing each of these individuals to the major's attention <\s>
<s> in one moment meejor i'm your humble servant and to dash into the little adjoining chamber where he slept to give a twist to his lank hair with his hair brush a wonderful and ancient piece to tear off his old stock and put on a new one which emily had constructed for him and to assume a handsome clean collar and the new coat which had been ordered upon the occasion of miss fotheringay's benefit was with the still active costigan the work of a minute <\s>
<s> after him sir derby entered and presently emerged from the same apartment where he also cased himself in his little shell jacket which fitted tightly upon the young officer's big person and which he and miss fotheringay and poor pen too perhaps admired prodigiously <\s>
<s> meanwhile conversation was engaged between the actress and the new comer and the usual remarks about the weather had been interchanged before costigan re entered in his new shoot as he called it <\s>
<s> i needn't apologoise to ye meejor he said in his richest and most courteous manner for receiving ye in me shirt sleeves <\s>
<s> an old soldier can't be better employed than in teaching a young one the use of his sword answered the major gallantly <\s>
<s> i remember in old times hearing that you could use yours pretty well captain costigan <\s>
<s> what ye've heard of jack costigan major said the other greatly <\s>
<s> the major had indeed he had pumped his nephew concerning his new friend the irish officer and whether he had no other knowledge of the captain than what he had thus gained or whether he actually remembered him we cannot say <\s>
<s> but major pendennis was a person of honour and undoubted veracity and said that he perfectly well recollected meeting mr <\s>
<s> costigan and hearing him sing at sir richard strachan's table at walcheren <\s>
<s> at this information and the bland and cordial manner in which it was conveyed bows looked up entirely puzzled <\s>
<s> but we will talk of these matters another time the major continued perhaps not wishing to commit himself it is to miss fotheringay that i came to pay my respects to day and he performed another bow for her so courtly and gracious that if she had been a duchess he could not have made it more handsome <\s>
<s> i had heard of your performances from my nephew madam the major said who raves about you as i believe you know pretty well <\s>
<s> but arthur is but a boy and a wild enthusiastic young fellow whose opinions one must not take au pied de la lettre and i confess i was anxious to judge for myself <\s>
<s> permit me to say your performance delighted and astonished me <\s>
<s> i have seen our best actresses and on my word i think you surpass them all <\s>
<s> you are as majestic as mrs <\s>
<s> faith i always said so costigan said winking at his daughter major take a chair <\s>
<s> milly rose at this hint took an uuripped satin garment off the only vacant seat and brought the latter to major pendennis with one of her finest curtseys <\s>
<s> you are as pathetic as miss o'neill he continued bowing and seating himself your snatches of song reminded me of mrs <\s>
<s> jordan in her best time when we were young men captain costigan and your manner reminded me of mars <\s>
<s> did you ever see the mars miss fotheringay <\s>
<s> there was two mahers in crow street remarked miss emily fanny was well enough but biddy was no great things <\s>
<s> sure the major means the god of war milly my dear interposed the parent <\s>
<s> it is not that mars i meant though venus i suppose may be pardoned for thinking about him the major replied with a smile directed in full to sir derby oaks who now re entered in his shell jacket but the lady did not understand the words of which he made use nor did the compliment at all pacify sir derby who probably did not understand it either and at any rate received it with great sulkiness and stiffness scowling uneasily at miss fotheringay with an expression which seemed to ask what the deuce does this man here <\s>
<s> major pendennis was not in the least annoyed by the gentleman's ill humour <\s>
<s> on the contrary it delighted him <\s>
<s> so thought he a rival is in the field and he offered up vows that sir derby might be not only a rival but a winner too in this love match in which he and pen were engaged <\s>
<s> i fear i interrupted your fencing lesson but my stay in chatteris is very short and i was anxious to make myself known to my old fellow campaigner captain costigan and to see a lady nearer who had charmed me so much from the stage <\s>
<s> i was not the only man epris last night miss fotheringay if i must call you so though your own family name is a very ancient and noble one <\s>
<s> there was a reverend friend of mine who went home in raptures with ophelia and i saw sir derby oaks fling a bouquet which no actress ever merited better <\s>
<s> i should have brought one myself had i known what i was going to see <\s>
<s> are not those the very flowers in a glass of water on the mantelpiece yonder <\s>
<s> i am very fond of flowers said miss fotheringay with a languishing ogle at sir derby oaks but the baronet still scowled sulkily <\s>
<s> sweets to the sweet isn't that the expression of the play <\s>
<s> pendennis asked bent upon being good humoured <\s>
<s> pon my life i don't know <\s>
<s> very likely it is <\s>
<s> i ain't much of a literary man answered sir derby <\s>
<s> the major continued with an air of surprise <\s>
<s> you don't inherit your father's love of letters then sir derby <\s>
<s> he was a remarkably fine scholar and i had the honour of knowing him very well <\s>
<s> indeed said the other and gave a sulky wag of his head <\s>
<s> he saved my life continued pendennis <\s>
<s> cried miss fotheringay rolling her eyes first upon the major with surprise then towards sir derby with gratitude but the latter was proof against those glances and far from appearing to be pleased that the apothecary his father should have saved major pendennis's life the young man actually looked as if he wished the event had turned the other way <\s>
<s> my father i believe was a very good doctor the young gentleman said by way of reply <\s>
<s> i'm not in that line myself <\s>
<s> i wish you good morning sir <\s>
<s> i've got an appointment cos bye bye miss fotheringay good morning <\s>
<s> and in spite of the young lady's imploring looks and appealing smiles the dragoon bowed stiffly out of the room and the clatter of his sabre was heard as he strode down the creaking stair and the angry tones of his voice as he cursed little tom creed who was disporting in the passage and whose peg top sir derby kicked away with an oath into the street <\s>
<s> the major did not smile in the least though he had every reason to be amused <\s>
<s> monstrous handsome young man that as fine a looking soldier as ever i saw he said to costigan <\s>
<s> a credit to the army and to human nature in general answered costigan <\s>
<s> a young man of refoined manners polite affabilitee and princely fortune <\s>
<s> his table is sumptuous he's adawr'd in the regiment and he rides sixteen stone <\s>
<s> a perfect champion said the major laughing <\s>
<s> i have no doubt all the ladies admire him <\s>
<s> he's very well in spite of his weight now he's young said milly but he's no conversation <\s>
<s> he's best on horseback mr <\s>
<s> bows said on which milly replied that the baronet had ridden third in the steeple chase on his horse tareaways and the major began to comprehend that the young lady herself was not of a particular genius and to wonder how she should be so stupid and act so well <\s>
<s> costigan with irish hospitality of course pressed refreshment upon his guest and the major who was no more hungry than you are after a lord mayor's dinner declared that he should like a biscuit and a glass of wine above all things as he felt quite faint from long fasting but he knew that to receive small kindnesses flatters the donors very much and that people must needs grow well disposed towards you as they give you their hospitality <\s>
<s> some of the old madara milly love costigan said winking to his child and that lady turning to her father a glance of intelligence went out of the room and down the stair where she softly summoned her little emissary master tommy creed and giving him a piece of money ordered him to go buy a pint of madara wine at the grapes and sixpennyworth of sorted biscuits at the baker's and to return in a hurry when he might have two biscuits for himself <\s>
<s> whilst tommy creed was gone on this errand miss costigan sate below with mrs <\s>
<s> creed telling her landlady how mr <\s>
<s> arthur pendennis's uncle the major was above stairs a nice soft spoken old gentleman that butter wouldn't melt in his mouth and how sir derby had gone out of the room in a rage of jealousy and thinking what must be done to pacify both of them <\s>
<s> she keeps the keys of the cellar major said mr <\s>
<s> costigan as the girl left the room <\s>
<s> upon my word you have a very beautiful butler answered pendennis gallantly and i don't wonder at the young fellows raving about her <\s>
<s> when we were of their age captain costigan i think plainer women would have done our business <\s>
<s> faith and ye may say that sir and lucky is the man who gets her <\s>
<s> ask me friend bob bows here whether miss fotheringay's moind is not even shuparior to her person and whether she does not possess a cultiveated intellect a refoined understanding and an emiable disposition <\s>
<s> o of course said mr <\s>
<s> here comes hebe blushing from the cellar <\s>
<s> don't you think it is time to go to rehearsal miss hebe <\s>
<s> you will be fined if you are later and he gave the young lady a look which intimated that they had much better leave the room and the two elders together <\s>
<s> at this order miss hebe took up her bonnet and shawl looking uncommonly pretty good humoured and smiling and bows gathered up his roll of papers and hobbled across the room for his hat and cane <\s>
<s> can't you give us a few minutes more miss fotheringay <\s>
<s> before you leave us permit an old fellow to shake you by the hand and believe that i am proud to have had the honour of making your acquaintance and am most sincerely anxious to be your friend <\s>
<s> miss fotheringay made a low curtsey at the conclusion of this gallant speech and the major followed her retreating steps to the door where he squeezed her hand with the kindest and most paternal pressure <\s>
<s> bows was puzzled with this exhibition of cordiality the lad's relatives can't be really wanting to marry him to her he thought and so they departed <\s>
<s> now for it thought major pendennis and as for mr <\s>
<s> costigan he profited instantaneously by his daughter's absence to drink up the rest of the wine and tossed off one bumper after another of the madeira from the grapes with an eager shaking hand <\s>
<s> the major came up to the table and took up his glass and drained it with a jovial smack <\s>
<s> if it had been lord steyne's particular and not public house cape he could not have appeared to relish it more <\s>
<s> capital madeira captain costigan he said <\s>
<s> where do you get it <\s>
<s> i drink the health of that charming creature in a bumper <\s>
<s> faith captain i don't wonder that the men are wild about her <\s>
<s> i never saw such eyes in my life or such a grand manner <\s>
<s> i am sure she is as intellectual as she is beautiful and i have no doubt she's as good as she is clever <\s>
<s> a good girl sir a good girl sir said the delighted father and i pledge a toast to her with all my heart <\s>
<s> shall i send to the to the cellar for another pint <\s>
<s> well indeed sir ye may say she is a good girl and the pride and glory of her father honest old jack costigan <\s>

<s> it is not that mars i meant though venus i suppose may be pardoned for thinking about him the major replied with a smile directed in full to sir derby oaks who now re entered in his shell jacket but the lady did not understand the words of which he made use nor did the compliment at all pacify sir derby who probably did not understand it either and at any rate received it with great sulkiness and stiffness scowling uneasily at miss fotheringay with an expression which seemed to ask what the deuce does this man here <\s>
<s> major pendennis was not in the least annoyed by the gentleman's ill humour <\s>
<s> on the contrary it delighted him <\s>
<s> so thought he a rival is in the field and he offered up vows that sir derby might be not only a rival but a winner too in this love match in which he and pen were engaged <\s>
<s> i fear i interrupted your fencing lesson but my stay in chatteris is very short and i was anxious to make myself known to my old fellow campaigner captain costigan and to see a lady nearer who had charmed me so much from the stage <\s>
<s> i was not the only man epris last night miss fotheringay if i must call you so though your own family name is a very ancient and noble one <\s>
<s> there was a reverend friend of mine who went home in raptures with ophelia and i saw sir derby oaks fling a bouquet which no actress ever merited better <\s>
<s> i should have brought one myself had i known what i was going to see <\s>
<s> are not those the very flowers in a glass of water on the mantelpiece yonder <\s>
<s> i am very fond of flowers said miss fotheringay with a languishing ogle at sir derby oaks but the baronet still scowled sulkily <\s>
<s> sweets to the sweet isn't that the expression of the play <\s>
<s> pendennis asked bent upon being good humoured <\s>
<s> pon my life i don't know <\s>
<s> very likely it is <\s>
<s> i ain't much of a literary man answered sir derby <\s>
<s> the major continued with an air of surprise <\s>
<s> you don't inherit your father's love of letters then sir derby <\s>
<s> he was a remarkably fine scholar and i had the honour of knowing him very well <\s>
<s> indeed said the other and gave a sulky wag of his head <\s>
<s> he saved my life continued pendennis <\s>
<s> cried miss fotheringay rolling her eyes first upon the major with surprise then towards sir derby with gratitude but the latter was proof against those glances and far from appearing to be pleased that the apothecary his father should have saved major pendennis's life the young man actually looked as if he wished the event had turned the other way <\s>
<s> my father i believe was a very good doctor the young gentleman said by way of reply <\s>
<s> i'm not in that line myself <\s>
<s> i wish you good morning sir <\s>
<s> i've got an appointment cos bye bye miss fotheringay good morning <\s>
<s> and in spite of the young lady's imploring looks and appealing smiles the dragoon bowed stiffly out of the room and the clatter of his sabre was heard as he strode down the creaking stair and the angry tones of his voice as he cursed little tom creed who was disporting in the passage and whose peg top sir derby kicked away with an oath into the street <\s>
<s> the major did not smile in the least though he had every reason to be amused <\s>
<s> monstrous handsome young man that as fine a looking soldier as ever i saw he said to costigan <\s>
<s> a credit to the army and to human nature in general answered costigan <\s>
<s> a young man of refoined manners polite affabilitee and princely fortune <\s>
<s> his table is sumptuous he's adawr'd in the regiment and he rides sixteen stone <\s>
<s> a perfect champion said the major laughing <\s>
<s> i have no doubt all the ladies admire him <\s>
<s> he's very well in spite of his weight now he's young said milly but he's no conversation <\s>
<s> he's best on horseback mr <\s>
<s> bows said on which milly replied that the baronet had ridden third in the steeple chase on his horse tareaways and the major began to comprehend that the young lady herself was not of a particular genius and to wonder how she should be so stupid and act so well <\s>
<s> costigan with irish hospitality of course pressed refreshment upon his guest and the major who was no more hungry than you are after a lord mayor's dinner declared that he should like a biscuit and a glass of wine above all things as he felt quite faint from long fasting but he knew that to receive small kindnesses flatters the donors very much and that people must needs grow well disposed towards you as they give you their hospitality <\s>
<s> some of the old madara milly love costigan said winking to his child and that lady turning to her father a glance of intelligence went out of the room and down the stair where she softly summoned her little emissary master tommy creed and giving him a piece of money ordered him to go buy a pint of madara wine at the grapes and sixpennyworth of sorted biscuits at the baker's and to return in a hurry when he might have two biscuits for himself <\s>
<s> whilst tommy creed was gone on this errand miss costigan sate below with mrs <\s>
<s> creed telling her landlady how mr <\s>
<s> arthur pendennis's uncle the major was above stairs a nice soft spoken old gentleman that butter wouldn't melt in his mouth and how sir derby had gone out of the room in a rage of jealousy and thinking what must be done to pacify both of them <\s>
<s> she keeps the keys of the cellar major said mr <\s>
<s> costigan as the girl left the room <\s>
<s> upon my word you have a very beautiful butler answered pendennis gallantly and i don't wonder at the young fellows raving about her <\s>
<s> when we were of their age captain costigan i think plainer women would have done our business <\s>
<s> faith and ye may say that sir and lucky is the man who gets her <\s>
<s> ask me friend bob bows here whether miss fotheringay's moind is not even shuparior to her person and whether she does not possess a cultiveated intellect a refoined understanding and an emiable disposition <\s>
<s> o of course said mr <\s>
<s> here comes hebe blushing from the cellar <\s>
<s> don't you think it is time to go to rehearsal miss hebe <\s>
<s> you will be fined if you are later and he gave the young lady a look which intimated that they had much better leave the room and the two elders together <\s>
<s> at this order miss hebe took up her bonnet and shawl looking uncommonly pretty good humoured and smiling and bows gathered up his roll of papers and hobbled across the room for his hat and cane <\s>
<s> can't you give us a few minutes more miss fotheringay <\s>
<s> before you leave us permit an old fellow to shake you by the hand and believe that i am proud to have had the honour of making your acquaintance and am most sincerely anxious to be your friend <\s>
<s> miss fotheringay made a low curtsey at the conclusion of this gallant speech and the major followed her retreating steps to the door where he squeezed her hand with the kindest and most paternal pressure <\s>
<s> bows was puzzled with this exhibition of cordiality the lad's relatives can't be really wanting to marry him to her he thought and so they departed <\s>
<s> now for it thought major pendennis and as for mr <\s>
<s> costigan he profited instantaneously by his daughter's absence to drink up the rest of the wine and tossed off one bumper after another of the madeira from the grapes with an eager shaking hand <\s>
<s> the major came up to the table and took up his glass and drained it with a jovial smack <\s>
<s> if it had been lord steyne's particular and not public house cape he could not have appeared to relish it more <\s>
<s> capital madeira captain costigan he said <\s>
<s> where do you get it <\s>
<s> i drink the health of that charming creature in a bumper <\s>
<s> faith captain i don't wonder that the men are wild about her <\s>
<s> i never saw such eyes in my life or such a grand manner <\s>
<s> i am sure she is as intellectual as she is beautiful and i have no doubt she's as good as she is clever <\s>
<s> a good girl sir a good girl sir said the delighted father and i pledge a toast to her with all my heart <\s>
<s> shall i send to the to the cellar for another pint <\s>
<s> well indeed sir ye may say she is a good girl and the pride and glory of her father honest old jack costigan <\s>
<s> the man who gets her will have a jew'l to a wife sir and i drink his health sir and ye know who i mean major <\s>
<s> i am not surprised at young or old falling in love with her said the major and frankly must tell you that though i was very angry with my poor nephew arthur when i heard of the boy's passion now i have seen the lady i can pardon him any extent of it <\s>
<s> by george i should like to enter for the race myself if i weren't an old fellow and a poor one <\s>
<s> and no better man major i'm sure cried jack enraptured <\s>
<s> the little crooked old man in the window seat who had been witnessing the fencing match between the two gentlemen whose stamping and jumping had been such as to cause him to give up all attempts to continue writing the theatre music in the copying of which he had been engaged looked up eagerly towards the new comer as the major of the well blacked boots entered the apartment distributing the most graceful bows to everybody present <\s>
<s> me daughter me friend mr <\s>
<s> bows me gallant young pupil and friend i may call um sir derby oaks said costigan splendidly waving his hand and pointing each of these individuals to the major's attention <\s>
<s> in one moment meejor i'm your humble servant and to dash into the little adjoining chamber where he slept to give a twist to his lank hair with his hair brush a wonderful and ancient piece to tear off his old stock and put on a new one which emily had constructed for him and to assume a handsome clean collar and the new coat which had been ordered upon the occasion of miss fotheringay's benefit was with the still active costigan the work of a minute <\s>
<s> after him sir derby entered and presently emerged from the same apartment where he also cased himself in his little shell jacket which fitted tightly upon the young officer's big person and which he and miss fotheringay and poor pen too perhaps admired prodigiously <\s>
<s> meanwhile conversation was engaged between the actress and the new comer and the usual remarks about the weather had been interchanged before costigan re entered in his new shoot as he called it <\s>
<s> i needn't apologoise to ye meejor he said in his richest and most courteous manner for receiving ye in me shirt sleeves <\s>
<s> an old soldier can't be better employed than in teaching a young one the use of his sword answered the major gallantly <\s>
<s> i remember in old times hearing that you could use yours pretty well captain costigan <\s>
<s> what ye've heard of jack costigan major said the other greatly <\s>
<s> the major had indeed he had pumped his nephew concerning his new friend the irish officer and whether he had no other knowledge of the captain than what he had thus gained or whether he actually remembered him we cannot say <\s>
<s> but major pendennis was a person of honour and undoubted veracity and said that he perfectly well recollected meeting mr <\s>
<s> costigan and hearing him sing at sir richard strachan's table at walcheren <\s>

<s> i had heard of your performances from my nephew madam the major said who raves about you as i believe you know pretty well <\s>

<s> a perfect champion said the major laughing <\s>
<s> i have no doubt all the ladies admire him <\s>
<s> he's very well in spite of his weight now he's young said milly but he's no conversation <\s>
<s> he's best on horseback mr <\s>
<s> bows said on which milly replied that the baronet had ridden third in the steeple chase on his horse tareaways and the major began to comprehend that the young lady herself was not of a particular genius and to wonder how she should be so stupid and act so well <\s>
<s> costigan with irish hospitality of course pressed refreshment upon his guest and the major who was no more hungry than you are after a lord mayor's dinner declared that he should like a biscuit and a glass of wine above all things as he felt quite faint from long fasting but he knew that to receive small kindnesses flatters the donors very much and that people must needs grow well disposed towards you as they give you their hospitality <\s>
<s> some of the old madara milly love costigan said winking to his child and that lady turning to her father a glance of intelligence went out of the room and down the stair where she softly summoned her little emissary master tommy creed and giving him a piece of money ordered him to go buy a pint of madara wine at the grapes and sixpennyworth of sorted biscuits at the baker's and to return in a hurry when he might have two biscuits for himself <\s>
<s> whilst tommy creed was gone on this errand miss costigan sate below with mrs <\s>
<s> creed telling her landlady how mr <\s>
<s> arthur pendennis's uncle the major was above stairs a nice soft spoken old gentleman that butter wouldn't melt in his mouth and how sir derby had gone out of the room in a rage of jealousy and thinking what must be done to pacify both of them <\s>
<s> she keeps the keys of the cellar major said mr <\s>
<s> costigan as the girl left the room <\s>
<s> upon my word you have a very beautiful butler answered pendennis gallantly and i don't wonder at the young fellows raving about her <\s>
<s> when we were of their age captain costigan i think plainer women would have done our business <\s>
<s> faith and ye may say that sir and lucky is the man who gets her <\s>
<s> ask me friend bob bows here whether miss fotheringay's moind is not even shuparior to her person and whether she does not possess a cultiveated intellect a refoined understanding and an emiable disposition <\s>
<s> o of course said mr <\s>
<s> here comes hebe blushing from the cellar <\s>
<s> don't you think it is time to go to rehearsal miss hebe <\s>
<s> you will be fined if you are later and he gave the young lady a look which intimated that they had much better leave the room and the two elders together <\s>
<s> at this order miss hebe took up her bonnet and shawl looking uncommonly pretty good humoured and smiling and bows gathered up his roll of papers and hobbled across the room for his hat and cane <\s>
<s> can't you give us a few minutes more miss fotheringay <\s>
<s> before you leave us permit an old fellow to shake you by the hand and believe that i am proud to have had the honour of making your acquaintance and am most sincerely anxious to be your friend <\s>
<s> miss fotheringay made a low curtsey at the conclusion of this gallant speech and the major followed her retreating steps to the door where he squeezed her hand with the kindest and most paternal pressure <\s>
<s> bows was puzzled with this exhibition of cordiality the lad's relatives can't be really wanting to marry him to her he thought and so they departed <\s>
<s> now for it thought major pendennis and as for mr <\s>
<s> costigan he profited instantaneously by his daughter's absence to drink up the rest of the wine and tossed off one bumper after another of the madeira from the grapes with an eager shaking hand <\s>
<s> the major came up to the table and took up his glass and drained it with a jovial smack <\s>
<s> if it had been lord steyne's particular and not public house cape he could not have appeared to relish it more <\s>
<s> capital madeira captain costigan he said <\s>
<s> where do you get it <\s>
<s> i drink the health of that charming creature in a bumper <\s>
<s> faith captain i don't wonder that the men are wild about her <\s>
<s> i never saw such eyes in my life or such a grand manner <\s>
<s> i am sure she is as intellectual as she is beautiful and i have no doubt she's as good as she is clever <\s>
<s> a good girl sir a good girl sir said the delighted father and i pledge a toast to her with all my heart <\s>
<s> shall i send to the to the cellar for another pint <\s>
<s> well indeed sir ye may say she is a good girl and the pride and glory of her father honest old jack costigan <\s>
<s> the man who gets her will have a jew'l to a wife sir and i drink his health sir and ye know who i mean major <\s>
<s> i am not surprised at young or old falling in love with her said the major and frankly must tell you that though i was very angry with my poor nephew arthur when i heard of the boy's passion now i have seen the lady i can pardon him any extent of it <\s>
<s> by george i should like to enter for the race myself if i weren't an old fellow and a poor one <\s>
<s> and no better man major i'm sure cried jack enraptured <\s>
<s> the little crooked old man in the window seat who had been witnessing the fencing match between the two gentlemen whose stamping and jumping had been such as to cause him to give up all attempts to continue writing the theatre music in the copying of which he had been engaged looked up eagerly towards the new comer as the major of the well blacked boots entered the apartment distributing the most graceful bows to everybody present <\s>
<s> me daughter me friend mr <\s>
<s> bows me gallant young pupil and friend i may call um sir derby oaks said costigan splendidly waving his hand and pointing each of these individuals to the major's attention <\s>
<s> in one moment meejor i'm your humble servant and to dash into the little adjoining chamber where he slept to give a twist to his lank hair with his hair brush a wonderful and ancient piece to tear off his old stock and put on a new one which emily had constructed for him and to assume a handsome clean collar and the new coat which had been ordered upon the occasion of miss fotheringay's benefit was with the still active costigan the work of a minute <\s>
<s> after him sir derby entered and presently emerged from the same apartment where he also cased himself in his little shell jacket which fitted tightly upon the young officer's big person and which he and miss fotheringay and poor pen too perhaps admired prodigiously <\s>
<s> meanwhile conversation was engaged between the actress and the new comer and the usual remarks about the weather had been interchanged before costigan re entered in his new shoot as he called it <\s>
<s> i needn't apologoise to ye meejor he said in his richest and most courteous manner for receiving ye in me shirt sleeves <\s>
<s> an old soldier can't be better employed than in teaching a young one the use of his sword answered the major gallantly <\s>
<s> i remember in old times hearing that you could use yours pretty well captain costigan <\s>
<s> what ye've heard of jack costigan major said the other greatly <\s>
<s> the major had indeed he had pumped his nephew concerning his new friend the irish officer and whether he had no other knowledge of the captain than what he had thus gained or whether he actually remembered him we cannot say <\s>
<s> but major pendennis was a person of honour and undoubted veracity and said that he perfectly well recollected meeting mr <\s>
<s> costigan and hearing him sing at sir richard strachan's table at walcheren <\s>
<s> at this information and the bland and cordial manner in which it was conveyed bows looked up entirely puzzled <\s>
<s> but we will talk of these matters another time the major continued perhaps not wishing to commit himself it is to miss fotheringay that i came to pay my respects to day and he performed another bow for her so courtly and gracious that if she had been a duchess he could not have made it more handsome <\s>
<s> i had heard of your performances from my nephew madam the major said who raves about you as i believe you know pretty well <\s>
<s> but arthur is but a boy and a wild enthusiastic young fellow whose opinions one must not take au pied de la lettre and i confess i was anxious to judge for myself <\s>
<s> permit me to say your performance delighted and astonished me <\s>
<s> i have seen our best actresses and on my word i think you surpass them all <\s>
<s> you are as majestic as mrs <\s>
<s> faith i always said so costigan said winking at his daughter major take a chair <\s>
<s> milly rose at this hint took an uuripped satin garment off the only vacant seat and brought the latter to major pendennis with one of her finest curtseys <\s>
<s> you are as pathetic as miss o'neill he continued bowing and seating himself your snatches of song reminded me of mrs <\s>
<s> jordan in her best time when we were young men captain costigan and your manner reminded me of mars <\s>
<s> did you ever see the mars miss fotheringay <\s>
<s> there was two mahers in crow street remarked miss emily fanny was well enough but biddy was no great things <\s>
<s> sure the major means the god of war milly my dear interposed the parent <\s>
<s> it is not that mars i meant though venus i suppose may be pardoned for thinking about him the major replied with a smile directed in full to sir derby oaks who now re entered in his shell jacket but the lady did not understand the words of which he made use nor did the compliment at all pacify sir derby who probably did not understand it either and at any rate received it with great sulkiness and stiffness scowling uneasily at miss fotheringay with an expression which seemed to ask what the deuce does this man here <\s>
<s> major pendennis was not in the least annoyed by the gentleman's ill humour <\s>
<s> on the contrary it delighted him <\s>
<s> so thought he a rival is in the field and he offered up vows that sir derby might be not only a rival but a winner too in this love match in which he and pen were engaged <\s>
<s> i fear i interrupted your fencing lesson but my stay in chatteris is very short and i was anxious to make myself known to my old fellow campaigner captain costigan and to see a lady nearer who had charmed me so much from the stage <\s>
<s> i was not the only man epris last night miss fotheringay if i must call you so though your own family name is a very ancient and noble one <\s>
<s> there was a reverend friend of mine who went home in raptures with ophelia and i saw sir derby oaks fling a bouquet which no actress ever merited better <\s>
<s> i should have brought one myself had i known what i was going to see <\s>
<s> are not those the very flowers in a glass of water on the mantelpiece yonder <\s>

<s> very likely it is <\s>

<s> the major came up to the table and took up his glass and drained it with a jovial smack <\s>
<s> if it had been lord steyne's particular and not public house cape he could not have appeared to relish it more <\s>

<s> where do you get it <\s>
<s> i drink the health of that charming creature in a bumper <\s>
<s> faith captain i don't wonder that the men are wild about her <\s>
<s> i never saw such eyes in my life or such a grand manner <\s>
<s> i am sure she is as intellectual as she is beautiful and i have no doubt she's as good as she is clever <\s>
<s> a good girl sir a good girl sir said the delighted father and i pledge a toast to her with all my heart <\s>
<s> shall i send to the to the cellar for another pint <\s>
<s> well indeed sir ye may say she is a good girl and the pride and glory of her father honest old jack costigan <\s>
<s> the man who gets her will have a jew'l to a wife sir and i drink his health sir and ye know who i mean major <\s>
<s> i am not surprised at young or old falling in love with her said the major and frankly must tell you that though i was very angry with my poor nephew arthur when i heard of the boy's passion now i have seen the lady i can pardon him any extent of it <\s>
<s> by george i should like to enter for the race myself if i weren't an old fellow and a poor one <\s>
<s> and no better man major i'm sure cried jack enraptured <\s>
<s> the little crooked old man in the window seat who had been witnessing the fencing match between the two gentlemen whose stamping and jumping had been such as to cause him to give up all attempts to continue writing the theatre music in the copying of which he had been engaged looked up eagerly towards the new comer as the major of the well blacked boots entered the apartment distributing the most graceful bows to everybody present <\s>
<s> me daughter me friend mr <\s>
<s> bows me gallant young pupil and friend i may call um sir derby oaks said costigan splendidly waving his hand and pointing each of these individuals to the major's attention <\s>
<s> in one moment meejor i'm your humble servant and to dash into the little adjoining chamber where he slept to give a twist to his lank hair with his hair brush a wonderful and ancient piece to tear off his old stock and put on a new one which emily had constructed for him and to assume a handsome clean collar and the new coat which had been ordered upon the occasion of miss fotheringay's benefit was with the still active costigan the work of a minute <\s>
<s> after him sir derby entered and presently emerged from the same apartment where he also cased himself in his little shell jacket which fitted tightly upon the young officer's big person and which he and miss fotheringay and poor pen too perhaps admired prodigiously <\s>
<s> meanwhile conversation was engaged between the actress and the new comer and the usual remarks about the weather had been interchanged before costigan re entered in his new shoot as he called it <\s>
<s> i needn't apologoise to ye meejor he said in his richest and most courteous manner for receiving ye in me shirt sleeves <\s>
<s> an old soldier can't be better employed than in teaching a young one the use of his sword answered the major gallantly <\s>
<s> i remember in old times hearing that you could use yours pretty well captain costigan <\s>
<s> what ye've heard of jack costigan major said the other greatly <\s>
<s> the major had indeed he had pumped his nephew concerning his new friend the irish officer and whether he had no other knowledge of the captain than what he had thus gained or whether he actually remembered him we cannot say <\s>
<s> but major pendennis was a person of honour and undoubted veracity and said that he perfectly well recollected meeting mr <\s>
<s> costigan and hearing him sing at sir richard strachan's table at walcheren <\s>
<s> at this information and the bland and cordial manner in which it was conveyed bows looked up entirely puzzled <\s>
<s> but we will talk of these matters another time the major continued perhaps not wishing to commit himself it is to miss fotheringay that i came to pay my respects to day and he performed another bow for her so courtly and gracious that if she had been a duchess he could not have made it more handsome <\s>
<s> i had heard of your performances from my nephew madam the major said who raves about you as i believe you know pretty well <\s>
<s> but arthur is but a boy and a wild enthusiastic young fellow whose opinions one must not take au pied de la lettre and i confess i was anxious to judge for myself <\s>
<s> permit me to say your performance delighted and astonished me <\s>
<s> i have seen our best actresses and on my word i think you surpass them all <\s>
<s> you are as majestic as mrs <\s>
<s> faith i always said so costigan said winking at his daughter major take a chair <\s>
<s> milly rose at this hint took an uuripped satin garment off the only vacant seat and brought the latter to major pendennis with one of her finest curtseys <\s>
<s> you are as pathetic as miss o'neill he continued bowing and seating himself your snatches of song reminded me of mrs <\s>
<s> jordan in her best time when we were young men captain costigan and your manner reminded me of mars <\s>
<s> did you ever see the mars miss fotheringay <\s>
<s> there was two mahers in crow street remarked miss emily fanny was well enough but biddy was no great things <\s>
<s> sure the major means the god of war milly my dear interposed the parent <\s>
<s> it is not that mars i meant though venus i suppose may be pardoned for thinking about him the major replied with a smile directed in full to sir derby oaks who now re entered in his shell jacket but the lady did not understand the words of which he made use nor did the compliment at all pacify sir derby who probably did not understand it either and at any rate received it with great sulkiness and stiffness scowling uneasily at miss fotheringay with an expression which seemed to ask what the deuce does this man here <\s>
<s> major pendennis was not in the least annoyed by the gentleman's ill humour <\s>
<s> on the contrary it delighted him <\s>
<s> so thought he a rival is in the field and he offered up vows that sir derby might be not only a rival but a winner too in this love match in which he and pen were engaged <\s>
<s> i fear i interrupted your fencing lesson but my stay in chatteris is very short and i was anxious to make myself known to my old fellow campaigner captain costigan and to see a lady nearer who had charmed me so much from the stage <\s>
<s> i was not the only man epris last night miss fotheringay if i must call you so though your own family name is a very ancient and noble one <\s>
<s> there was a reverend friend of mine who went home in raptures with ophelia and i saw sir derby oaks fling a bouquet which no actress ever merited better <\s>
<s> i should have brought one myself had i known what i was going to see <\s>
<s> are not those the very flowers in a glass of water on the mantelpiece yonder <\s>
<s> i am very fond of flowers said miss fotheringay with a languishing ogle at sir derby oaks but the baronet still scowled sulkily <\s>
<s> sweets to the sweet isn't that the expression of the play <\s>
<s> pendennis asked bent upon being good humoured <\s>
<s> pon my life i don't know <\s>
<s> very likely it is <\s>
<s> i ain't much of a literary man answered sir derby <\s>
<s> the major continued with an air of surprise <\s>
<s> you don't inherit your father's love of letters then sir derby <\s>
<s> he was a remarkably fine scholar and i had the honour of knowing him very well <\s>
<s> indeed said the other and gave a sulky wag of his head <\s>
<s> he saved my life continued pendennis <\s>
<s> cried miss fotheringay rolling her eyes first upon the major with surprise then towards sir derby with gratitude but the latter was proof against those glances and far from appearing to be pleased that the apothecary his father should have saved major pendennis's life the young man actually looked as if he wished the event had turned the other way <\s>
<s> my father i believe was a very good doctor the young gentleman said by way of reply <\s>
<s> i'm not in that line myself <\s>
<s> i wish you good morning sir <\s>
<s> i've got an appointment cos bye bye miss fotheringay good morning <\s>
<s> and in spite of the young lady's imploring looks and appealing smiles the dragoon bowed stiffly out of the room and the clatter of his sabre was heard as he strode down the creaking stair and the angry tones of his voice as he cursed little tom creed who was disporting in the passage and whose peg top sir derby kicked away with an oath into the street <\s>
<s> the major did not smile in the least though he had every reason to be amused <\s>
<s> monstrous handsome young man that as fine a looking soldier as ever i saw he said to costigan <\s>
<s> a credit to the army and to human nature in general answered costigan <\s>
<s> a young man of refoined manners polite affabilitee and princely fortune <\s>
<s> his table is sumptuous he's adawr'd in the regiment and he rides sixteen stone <\s>
<s> a perfect champion said the major laughing <\s>
<s> i have no doubt all the ladies admire him <\s>
<s> he's very well in spite of his weight now he's young said milly but he's no conversation <\s>
<s> he's best on horseback mr <\s>
<s> bows said on which milly replied that the baronet had ridden third in the steeple chase on his horse tareaways and the major began to comprehend that the young lady herself was not of a particular genius and to wonder how she should be so stupid and act so well <\s>
<s> costigan with irish hospitality of course pressed refreshment upon his guest and the major who was no more hungry than you are after a lord mayor's dinner declared that he should like a biscuit and a glass of wine above all things as he felt quite faint from long fasting but he knew that to receive small kindnesses flatters the donors very much and that people must needs grow well disposed towards you as they give you their hospitality <\s>
<s> some of the old madara milly love costigan said winking to his child and that lady turning to her father a glance of intelligence went out of the room and down the stair where she softly summoned her little emissary master tommy creed and giving him a piece of money ordered him to go buy a pint of madara wine at the grapes and sixpennyworth of sorted biscuits at the baker's and to return in a hurry when he might have two biscuits for himself <\s>

<s> costigan and hearing him sing at sir richard strachan's table at walcheren <\s>
<s> at this information and the bland and cordial manner in which it was conveyed bows looked up entirely puzzled <\s>
<s> but we will talk of these matters another time the major continued perhaps not wishing to commit himself it is to miss fotheringay that i came to pay my respects to day and he performed another bow for her so courtly and gracious that if she had been a duchess he could not have made it more handsome <\s>
<s> i had heard of your performances from my nephew madam the major said who raves about you as i believe you know pretty well <\s>
<s> but arthur is but a boy and a wild enthusiastic young fellow whose opinions one must not take au pied de la lettre and i confess i was anxious to judge for myself <\s>
<s> permit me to say your performance delighted and astonished me <\s>
<s> i have seen our best actresses and on my word i think you surpass them all <\s>
<s> you are as majestic as mrs <\s>
<s> faith i always said so costigan said winking at his daughter major take a chair <\s>
<s> milly rose at this hint took an uuripped satin garment off the only vacant seat and brought the latter to major pendennis with one of her finest curtseys <\s>
<s> you are as pathetic as miss o'neill he continued bowing and seating himself your snatches of song reminded me of mrs <\s>
<s> jordan in her best time when we were young men captain costigan and your manner reminded me of mars <\s>
<s> did you ever see the mars miss fotheringay <\s>
<s> there was two mahers in crow street remarked miss emily fanny was well enough but biddy was no great things <\s>
<s> sure the major means the god of war milly my dear interposed the parent <\s>
<s> it is not that mars i meant though venus i suppose may be pardoned for thinking about him the major replied with a smile directed in full to sir derby oaks who now re entered in his shell jacket but the lady did not understand the words of which he made use nor did the compliment at all pacify sir derby who probably did not understand it either and at any rate received it with great sulkiness and stiffness scowling uneasily at miss fotheringay with an expression which seemed to ask what the deuce does this man here <\s>
<s> major pendennis was not in the least annoyed by the gentleman's ill humour <\s>
<s> on the contrary it delighted him <\s>
<s> so thought he a rival is in the field and he offered up vows that sir derby might be not only a rival but a winner too in this love match in which he and pen were engaged <\s>
<s> i fear i interrupted your fencing lesson but my stay in chatteris is very short and i was anxious to make myself known to my old fellow campaigner captain costigan and to see a lady nearer who had charmed me so much from the stage <\s>
<s> i was not the only man epris last night miss fotheringay if i must call you so though your own family name is a very ancient and noble one <\s>
<s> there was a reverend friend of mine who went home in raptures with ophelia and i saw sir derby oaks fling a bouquet which no actress ever merited better <\s>
<s> i should have brought one myself had i known what i was going to see <\s>
<s> are not those the very flowers in a glass of water on the mantelpiece yonder <\s>
<s> i am very fond of flowers said miss fotheringay with a languishing ogle at sir derby oaks but the baronet still scowled sulkily <\s>
<s> sweets to the sweet isn't that the expression of the play <\s>
<s> pendennis asked bent upon being good humoured <\s>
<s> pon my life i don't know <\s>
<s> very likely it is <\s>
<s> i ain't much of a literary man answered sir derby <\s>
<s> the major continued with an air of surprise <\s>
<s> you don't inherit your father's love of letters then sir derby <\s>
<s> he was a remarkably fine scholar and i had the honour of knowing him very well <\s>
<s> indeed said the other and gave a sulky wag of his head <\s>
<s> he saved my life continued pendennis <\s>
<s> cried miss fotheringay rolling her eyes first upon the major with surprise then towards sir derby with gratitude but the latter was proof against those glances and far from appearing to be pleased that the apothecary his father should have saved major pendennis's life the young man actually looked as if he wished the event had turned the other way <\s>
<s> my father i believe was a very good doctor the young gentleman said by way of reply <\s>
<s> i'm not in that line myself <\s>
<s> i wish you good morning sir <\s>
<s> i've got an appointment cos bye bye miss fotheringay good morning <\s>
<s> and in spite of the young lady's imploring looks and appealing smiles the dragoon bowed stiffly out of the room and the clatter of his sabre was heard as he strode down the creaking stair and the angry tones of his voice as he cursed little tom creed who was disporting in the passage and whose peg top sir derby kicked away with an oath into the street <\s>
<s> the major did not smile in the least though he had every reason to be amused <\s>
<s> monstrous handsome young man that as fine a looking soldier as ever i saw he said to costigan <\s>
<s> a credit to the army and to human nature in general answered costigan <\s>
<s> a young man of refoined manners polite affabilitee and princely fortune <\s>
<s> his table is sumptuous he's adawr'd in the regiment and he rides sixteen stone <\s>
<s> a perfect champion said the major laughing <\s>
<s> i have no doubt all the ladies admire him <\s>
<s> he's very well in spite of his weight now he's young said milly but he's no conversation <\s>
<s> he's best on horseback mr <\s>
<s> bows said on which milly replied that the baronet had ridden third in the steeple chase on his horse tareaways and the major began to comprehend that the young lady herself was not of a particular genius and to wonder how she should be so stupid and act so well <\s>
<s> costigan with irish hospitality of course pressed refreshment upon his guest and the major who was no more hungry than you are after a lord mayor's dinner declared that he should like a biscuit and a glass of wine above all things as he felt quite faint from long fasting but he knew that to receive small kindnesses flatters the donors very much and that people must needs grow well disposed towards you as they give you their hospitality <\s>
<s> some of the old madara milly love costigan said winking to his child and that lady turning to her father a glance of intelligence went out of the room and down the stair where she softly summoned her little emissary master tommy creed and giving him a piece of money ordered him to go buy a pint of madara wine at the grapes and sixpennyworth of sorted biscuits at the baker's and to return in a hurry when he might have two biscuits for himself <\s>
<s> whilst tommy creed was gone on this errand miss costigan sate below with mrs <\s>
<s> creed telling her landlady how mr <\s>
<s> arthur pendennis's uncle the major was above stairs a nice soft spoken old gentleman that butter wouldn't melt in his mouth and how sir derby had gone out of the room in a rage of jealousy and thinking what must be done to pacify both of them <\s>
<s> she keeps the keys of the cellar major said mr <\s>
<s> costigan as the girl left the room <\s>
<s> upon my word you have a very beautiful butler answered pendennis gallantly and i don't wonder at the young fellows raving about her <\s>
<s> when we were of their age captain costigan i think plainer women would have done our business <\s>
<s> faith and ye may say that sir and lucky is the man who gets her <\s>
<s> ask me friend bob bows here whether miss fotheringay's moind is not even shuparior to her person and whether she does not possess a cultiveated intellect a refoined understanding and an emiable disposition <\s>
<s> o of course said mr <\s>
<s> here comes hebe blushing from the cellar <\s>
<s> don't you think it is time to go to rehearsal miss hebe <\s>
<s> you will be fined if you are later and he gave the young lady a look which intimated that they had much better leave the room and the two elders together <\s>
<s> at this order miss hebe took up her bonnet and shawl looking uncommonly pretty good humoured and smiling and bows gathered up his roll of papers and hobbled across the room for his hat and cane <\s>
<s> can't you give us a few minutes more miss fotheringay <\s>
<s> before you leave us permit an old fellow to shake you by the hand and believe that i am proud to have had the honour of making your acquaintance and am most sincerely anxious to be your friend <\s>
<s> miss fotheringay made a low curtsey at the conclusion of this gallant speech and the major followed her retreating steps to the door where he squeezed her hand with the kindest and most paternal pressure <\s>
<s> bows was puzzled with this exhibition of cordiality the lad's relatives can't be really wanting to marry him to her he thought and so they departed <\s>
<s> now for it thought major pendennis and as for mr <\s>
<s> costigan he profited instantaneously by his daughter's absence to drink up the rest of the wine and tossed off one bumper after another of the madeira from the grapes with an eager shaking hand <\s>
<s> the major came up to the table and took up his glass and drained it with a jovial smack <\s>
<s> if it had been lord steyne's particular and not public house cape he could not have appeared to relish it more <\s>
<s> capital madeira captain costigan he said <\s>
<s> where do you get it <\s>
<s> i drink the health of that charming creature in a bumper <\s>
<s> faith captain i don't wonder that the men are wild about her <\s>
<s> i never saw such eyes in my life or such a grand manner <\s>
<s> i am sure she is as intellectual as she is beautiful and i have no doubt she's as good as she is clever <\s>
<s> a good girl sir a good girl sir said the delighted father and i pledge a toast to her with all my heart <\s>
<s> shall i send to the to the cellar for another pint <\s>
<s> well indeed sir ye may say she is a good girl and the pride and glory of her father honest old jack costigan <\s>
<s> the man who gets her will have a jew'l to a wife sir and i drink his health sir and ye know who i mean major <\s>
<s> i am not surprised at young or old falling in love with her said the major and frankly must tell you that though i was very angry with my poor nephew arthur when i heard of the boy's passion now i have seen the lady i can pardon him any extent of it <\s>
<s> by george i should like to enter for the race myself if i weren't an old fellow and a poor one <\s>
<s> and no better man major i'm sure cried jack enraptured <\s>
<s> the little crooked old man in the window seat who had been witnessing the fencing match between the two gentlemen whose stamping and jumping had been such as to cause him to give up all attempts to continue writing the theatre music in the copying of which he had been engaged looked up eagerly towards the new comer as the major of the well blacked boots entered the apartment distributing the most graceful bows to everybody present <\s>
<s> me daughter me friend mr <\s>
<s> bows me gallant young pupil and friend i may call um sir derby oaks said costigan splendidly waving his hand and pointing each of these individuals to the major's attention <\s>
<s> in one moment meejor i'm your humble servant and to dash into the little adjoining chamber where he slept to give a twist to his lank hair with his hair brush a wonderful and ancient piece to tear off his old stock and put on a new one which emily had constructed for him and to assume a handsome clean collar and the new coat which had been ordered upon the occasion of miss fotheringay's benefit was with the still active costigan the work of a minute <\s>
<s> after him sir derby entered and presently emerged from the same apartment where he also cased himself in his little shell jacket which fitted tightly upon the young officer's big person and which he and miss fotheringay and poor pen too perhaps admired prodigiously <\s>

<s> i ain't much of a literary man answered sir derby <\s>
<s> the major continued with an air of surprise <\s>
<s> you don't inherit your father's love of letters then sir derby <\s>
<s> he was a remarkably fine scholar and i had the honour of knowing him very well <\s>
<s> indeed said the other and gave a sulky wag of his head <\s>
<s> he saved my life continued pendennis <\s>
<s> cried miss fotheringay rolling her eyes first upon the major with surprise then towards sir derby with gratitude but the latter was proof against those glances and far from appearing to be pleased that the apothecary his father should have saved major pendennis's life the young man actually looked as if he wished the event had turned the other way <\s>
<s> my father i believe was a very good doctor the young gentleman said by way of reply <\s>
<s> i'm not in that line myself <\s>
<s> i wish you good morning sir <\s>
<s> i've got an appointment cos bye bye miss fotheringay good morning <\s>
<s> and in spite of the young lady's imploring looks and appealing smiles the dragoon bowed stiffly out of the room and the clatter of his sabre was heard as he strode down the creaking stair and the angry tones of his voice as he cursed little tom creed who was disporting in the passage and whose peg top sir derby kicked away with an oath into the street <\s>
<s> the major did not smile in the least though he had every reason to be amused <\s>
<s> monstrous handsome young man that as fine a looking soldier as ever i saw he said to costigan <\s>
<s> a credit to the army and to human nature in general answered costigan <\s>
<s> a young man of refoined manners polite affabilitee and princely fortune <\s>
<s> his table is sumptuous he's adawr'd in the regiment and he rides sixteen stone <\s>
<s> a perfect champion said the major laughing <\s>
<s> i have no doubt all the ladies admire him <\s>
<s> he's very well in spite of his weight now he's young said milly but he's no conversation <\s>
<s> he's best on horseback mr <\s>
<s> bows said on which milly replied that the baronet had ridden third in the steeple chase on his horse tareaways and the major began to comprehend that the young lady herself was not of a particular genius and to wonder how she should be so stupid and act so well <\s>
<s> costigan with irish hospitality of course pressed refreshment upon his guest and the major who was no more hungry than you are after a lord mayor's dinner declared that he should like a biscuit and a glass of wine above all things as he felt quite faint from long fasting but he knew that to receive small kindnesses flatters the donors very much and that people must needs grow well disposed towards you as they give you their hospitality <\s>
<s> some of the old madara milly love costigan said winking to his child and that lady turning to her father a glance of intelligence went out of the room and down the stair where she softly summoned her little emissary master tommy creed and giving him a piece of money ordered him to go buy a pint of madara wine at the grapes and sixpennyworth of sorted biscuits at the baker's and to return in a hurry when he might have two biscuits for himself <\s>
<s> whilst tommy creed was gone on this errand miss costigan sate below with mrs <\s>
<s> creed telling her landlady how mr <\s>
<s> arthur pendennis's uncle the major was above stairs a nice soft spoken old gentleman that butter wouldn't melt in his mouth and how sir derby had gone out of the room in a rage of jealousy and thinking what must be done to pacify both of them <\s>
<s> she keeps the keys of the cellar major said mr <\s>
<s> costigan as the girl left the room <\s>
<s> upon my word you have a very beautiful butler answered pendennis gallantly and i don't wonder at the young fellows raving about her <\s>
<s> when we were of their age captain costigan i think plainer women would have done our business <\s>
<s> faith and ye may say that sir and lucky is the man who gets her <\s>
<s> ask me friend bob bows here whether miss fotheringay's moind is not even shuparior to her person and whether she does not possess a cultiveated intellect a refoined understanding and an emiable disposition <\s>
<s> o of course said mr <\s>
<s> here comes hebe blushing from the cellar <\s>
<s> don't you think it is time to go to rehearsal miss hebe <\s>
<s> you will be fined if you are later and he gave the young lady a look which intimated that they had much better leave the room and the two elders together <\s>
<s> at this order miss hebe took up her bonnet and shawl looking uncommonly pretty good humoured and smiling and bows gathered up his roll of papers and hobbled across the room for his hat and cane <\s>
<s> can't you give us a few minutes more miss fotheringay <\s>
<s> before you leave us permit an old fellow to shake you by the hand and believe that i am proud to have had the honour of making your acquaintance and am most sincerely anxious to be your friend <\s>
<s> miss fotheringay made a low curtsey at the conclusion of this gallant speech and the major followed her retreating steps to the door where he squeezed her hand with the kindest and most paternal pressure <\s>
<s> bows was puzzled with this exhibition of cordiality the lad's relatives can't be really wanting to marry him to her he thought and so they departed <\s>
<s> now for it thought major pendennis and as for mr <\s>
<s> costigan he profited instantaneously by his daughter's absence to drink up the rest of the wine and tossed off one bumper after another of the madeira from the grapes with an eager shaking hand <\s>
<s> the major came up to the table and took up his glass and drained it with a jovial smack <\s>
<s> if it had been lord steyne's particular and not public house cape he could not have appeared to relish it more <\s>
<s> capital madeira captain costigan he said <\s>
<s> where do you get it <\s>
<s> i drink the health of that charming creature in a bumper <\s>
<s> faith captain i don't wonder that the men are wild about her <\s>
<s> i never saw such eyes in my life or such a grand manner <\s>
<s> i am sure she is as intellectual as she is beautiful and i have no doubt she's as good as she is clever <\s>
<s> a good girl sir a good girl sir said the delighted father and i pledge a toast to her with all my heart <\s>
<s> shall i send to the to the cellar for another pint <\s>
<s> well indeed sir ye may say she is a good girl and the pride and glory of her father honest old jack costigan <\s>
<s> the man who gets her will have a jew'l to a wife sir and i drink his health sir and ye know who i mean major <\s>
<s> i am not surprised at young or old falling in love with her said the major and frankly must tell you that though i was very angry with my poor nephew arthur when i heard of the boy's passion now i have seen the lady i can pardon him any extent of it <\s>
<s> by george i should like to enter for the race myself if i weren't an old fellow and a poor one <\s>
<s> and no better man major i'm sure cried jack enraptured <\s>
<s> the little crooked old man in the window seat who had been witnessing the fencing match between the two gentlemen whose stamping and jumping had been such as to cause him to give up all attempts to continue writing the theatre music in the copying of which he had been engaged looked up eagerly towards the new comer as the major of the well blacked boots entered the apartment distributing the most graceful bows to everybody present <\s>
<s> me daughter me friend mr <\s>
<s> bows me gallant young pupil and friend i may call um sir derby oaks said costigan splendidly waving his hand and pointing each of these individuals to the major's attention <\s>
<s> in one moment meejor i'm your humble servant and to dash into the little adjoining chamber where he slept to give a twist to his lank hair with his hair brush a wonderful and ancient piece to tear off his old stock and put on a new one which emily had constructed for him and to assume a handsome clean collar and the new coat which had been ordered upon the occasion of miss fotheringay's benefit was with the still active costigan the work of a minute <\s>
<s> after him sir derby entered and presently emerged from the same apartment where he also cased himself in his little shell jacket which fitted tightly upon the young officer's big person and which he and miss fotheringay and poor pen too perhaps admired prodigiously <\s>
<s> meanwhile conversation was engaged between the actress and the new comer and the usual remarks about the weather had been interchanged before costigan re entered in his new shoot as he called it <\s>
<s> i needn't apologoise to ye meejor he said in his richest and most courteous manner for receiving ye in me shirt sleeves <\s>
<s> an old soldier can't be better employed than in teaching a young one the use of his sword answered the major gallantly <\s>
<s> i remember in old times hearing that you could use yours pretty well captain costigan <\s>
<s> what ye've heard of jack costigan major said the other greatly <\s>
<s> the major had indeed he had pumped his nephew concerning his new friend the irish officer and whether he had no other knowledge of the captain than what he had thus gained or whether he actually remembered him we cannot say <\s>
<s> but major pendennis was a person of honour and undoubted veracity and said that he perfectly well recollected meeting mr <\s>
<s> costigan and hearing him sing at sir richard strachan's table at walcheren <\s>
<s> at this information and the bland and cordial manner in which it was conveyed bows looked up entirely puzzled <\s>
<s> but we will talk of these matters another time the major continued perhaps not wishing to commit himself it is to miss fotheringay that i came to pay my respects to day and he performed another bow for her so courtly and gracious that if she had been a duchess he could not have made it more handsome <\s>
<s> i had heard of your performances from my nephew madam the major said who raves about you as i believe you know pretty well <\s>
<s> but arthur is but a boy and a wild enthusiastic young fellow whose opinions one must not take au pied de la lettre and i confess i was anxious to judge for myself <\s>
<s> permit me to say your performance delighted and astonished me <\s>
<s> i have seen our best actresses and on my word i think you surpass them all <\s>
<s> you are as majestic as mrs <\s>
<s> faith i always said so costigan said winking at his daughter major take a chair <\s>
<s> milly rose at this hint took an uuripped satin garment off the only vacant seat and brought the latter to major pendennis with one of her finest curtseys <\s>
<s> you are as pathetic as miss o'neill he continued bowing and seating himself your snatches of song reminded me of mrs <\s>
<s> jordan in her best time when we were young men captain costigan and your manner reminded me of mars <\s>
<s> did you ever see the mars miss fotheringay <\s>
<s> there was two mahers in crow street remarked miss emily fanny was well enough but biddy was no great things <\s>
<s> sure the major means the god of war milly my dear interposed the parent <\s>
<s> it is not that mars i meant though venus i suppose may be pardoned for thinking about him the major replied with a smile directed in full to sir derby oaks who now re entered in his shell jacket but the lady did not understand the words of which he made use nor did the compliment at all pacify sir derby who probably did not understand it either and at any rate received it with great sulkiness and stiffness scowling uneasily at miss fotheringay with an expression which seemed to ask what the deuce does this man here <\s>
<s> major pendennis was not in the least annoyed by the gentleman's ill humour <\s>
<s> on the contrary it delighted him <\s>
<s> so thought he a rival is in the field and he offered up vows that sir derby might be not only a rival but a winner too in this love match in which he and pen were engaged <\s>
<s> i fear i interrupted your fencing lesson but my stay in chatteris is very short and i was anxious to make myself known to my old fellow campaigner captain costigan and to see a lady nearer who had charmed me so much from the stage <\s>

<s> when we were of their age captain costigan i think plainer women would have done our business <\s>
<s> faith and ye may say that sir and lucky is the man who gets her <\s>
<s> ask me friend bob bows here whether miss fotheringay's moind is not even shuparior to her person and whether she does not possess a cultiveated intellect a refoined understanding and an emiable disposition <\s>
<s> o of course said mr <\s>
<s> here comes hebe blushing from the cellar <\s>
<s> don't you think it is time to go to rehearsal miss hebe <\s>
<s> you will be fined if you are later and he gave the young lady a look which intimated that they had much better leave the room and the two elders together <\s>
<s> at this order miss hebe took up her bonnet and shawl looking uncommonly pretty good humoured and smiling and bows gathered up his roll of papers and hobbled across the room for his hat and cane <\s>
<s> can't you give us a few minutes more miss fotheringay <\s>
<s> before you leave us permit an old fellow to shake you by the hand and believe that i am proud to have had the honour of making your acquaintance and am most sincerely anxious to be your friend <\s>
<s> miss fotheringay made a low curtsey at the conclusion of this gallant speech and the major followed her retreating steps to the door where he squeezed her hand with the kindest and most paternal pressure <\s>
<s> bows was puzzled with this exhibition of cordiality the lad's relatives can't be really wanting to marry him to her he thought and so they departed <\s>
<s> now for it thought major pendennis and as for mr <\s>
<s> costigan he profited instantaneously by his daughter's absence to drink up the rest of the wine and tossed off one bumper after another of the madeira from the grapes with an eager shaking hand <\s>
<s> the major came up to the table and took up his glass and drained it with a jovial smack <\s>
<s> if it had been lord steyne's particular and not public house cape he could not have appeared to relish it more <\s>
